Foreign Telegrams

Japan Confirms Its Policy Towards the League of Nations

No Intervention Allowed in the Recognition of Puppet Organizations

Intentionally Releasing League Exit Air to Intimidate the League of Nations

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Although European and American countries are currently silent on Japan's recognition of Manchuria, they are focusing all their efforts on the League of Nations General Assembly. The Japanese government, from Prime Minister Saitō to Foreign Minister Uchida, Army Minister Araki, Ambassador Debuchi, Participant Yoshida, and other officials, is collecting information from all sides and discussing countermeasures. Its fundamental policy has reportedly been determined as follows: (1) The independence of "Manchukuo" and the recognition of "Manchukuo" do not violate international treaties and are faits accomplis. They cannot be canceled or changed by a resolution of fifty-three to one. Furthermore, if the League of Nations attempts to cancel Japan's recognition, it would be suppressing Japan's sovereignty, which will be absolutely opposed. (2) Japan will absolutely oppose the application of Article 15 of the League Covenant to the Sino-Japanese dispute. Although Japan expresses overall opposition to the convening of a special general assembly, considering past relations, it will send Japanese representatives to attend as explainers to ensure that the worst possible outcome does not occur with the League of Nations. (3) If the League of Nations disregards Japan's claims, denies the independence of Manchukuo, and uses a 52-to-1 resolution to suppress Japan's legitimate claims, Japan will not only withdraw its delegation from the League of Nations but will also withdraw from the League of Nations altogether, and the responsibility for this will lie entirely with the League of Nations' obstinacy.

Reuters 18th, Tokyo: Foreign Ministry officials are currently considering what attitude Japan should take towards the Sino-Japanese dispute being discussed at next month's League of Nations General Assembly. It is now hoped that the League of Nations will understand Japan's position and prevent the situation from becoming more serious. Influential newspapers such as the Kokumin Shimbun have stated that if the League of Nations forces Japan to withdraw its recognition of "Manchukuo" or denies the independence of "Manchukuo," the result will be Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations. No matter what the League of Nations decides, Japan will never withdraw this recognition, because Japan's recognition and the independence of "Manchukuo" do not violate any treaties.

The League of Nations Worries About the Far East Situation

Our Protest to Japan Delivered to Geneva

The United States Accepts Our Note but Remains Silent for the Time Being

Reuters 18th, London: The League of Nations' concerns about the Far East situation and Germany's refusal to continue participating in the disarmament conference are the two major events noted by today's Sunday newspapers. An editorial in The Observer states that if the situation in Western Europe is causing anxiety to the League of Nations, this anxiety will be further exacerbated by the situation in the Far East. Today's question is whether the League of Nations can persuade Japan to remain a member. If Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, the damage will be borne by Geneva, not Tokyo. It also states that the League of Nations will no longer be concerned about the Far East issue because Soviet Russia and the United States are not members of the League of Nations, and China is a difficult country to grasp. The Sunday Times strongly advocates that Great Britain should take a more proactive policy, stating that Japan's actions are a major hazard for both economic and military reasons. If we do not dare to act effectively to deal with it now, the opportunity for disarmament will be greatly weakened. In addition, the United States is currently looking forward to Britain taking a proactive policy. If Britain remains silent, the war debt agreement, which has already been jeopardized by the failure of disarmament, will be greatly reduced in its chances of success due to misunderstandings between the two countries.

Kokuminsha 17th, Geneva: China's telegram protesting Japan's recognition of the puppet organization in the Northeast and the Japanese government's telegram notifying the League of Nations of the contents of the agreements signed between Japan and the puppet organization arrived in Geneva today at the same time. The Chinese government's telegram was addressed to the President of the League of Nations General Assembly and will be distributed to the member states before being released. The Japanese telegram was merely a notification and did not request registration with the League of Nations.

Kokuminsha 17th, Washington: Today, the Chinese legation published a document from the Chinese government to the United States denouncing Japan's violation of the Nine-Power Treaty. However, according to a certain gentleman within the US government, the United States is still waiting and does not intend to take immediate action.

Japan Tries Hard to Entice Soviet Russia

To Recognize the Puppet Organization

Far East News Agency 18th, Tokyo: The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that the attitude of Soviet Russia towards Manchuria is very important, so it has tried hard to entice it to recognize the puppet state of Manchukuo, seeking friendship between Japan and Russia and jointly building East Asia. However, Soviet Russia believes that the Japanese government's move is merely to realize its ambitions to invade Manchuria and is not sincere. Therefore, it also proposed that a non-aggression treaty between Japan and Russia must first be signed before it can agree. The Japanese side believes that such conditions are difficult to achieve, so there has been no result.

September 18th Anniversary

Japan Celebrates, We Mourn

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Today is the anniversary of the outbreak of the Manchurian Incident. From 10:00 AM, the Japanese residents of Shenyang held flag parades with approximately 10,000 people from various schools, citizens, and organizations. Veterans rode in 40 trucks to parade through the city. In the evening, tens of thousands of citizens held lantern parades. The puppet state also held flag parades from 10:00 AM by students and citizens. The flag parades of the Japanese and the puppet state met in front of the military headquarters. Lectures and celebration meetings were held in various places, with tens of thousands of people in attendance.

Japan Alliance News Agency 18th, Tokyo: Today, various memorial meetings were held in Tokyo to commemorate the day of the attack on Beidaying in Shenyang. At 12:30 PM, a memorial meeting was held at the Municipal First Middle School. After Lieutenant General Honjō and Brigade Commander Mori lectured on the Manchurian issue, a film of the Manchurian Incident was shown. At 6:30 PM, Lieutenant General Honjō, Tokyo Mayor Nagata, made radio speeches. At 8:30 PM, Plenipotentiary Mutō broadcast a speech from the Shenyang radio station. At 9:59 PM, the entire nation observed 30 seconds of silence to commemorate the fallen soldiers. The army authorities selected some soldiers who participated in the war to travel to various parts of the country to give speeches. Women's groups of army and navy officers, imperial military lecture groups, veterans associations, patriotic women's associations, etc., held memorial services, entertained bereaved families and wounded soldiers, and presented souvenirs. The Tokyo Prefecture and the municipal authorities held a welcome meeting for Lieutenant General Honjō at the Hibiya Public Hall.

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Today at 8:00 AM, Japanese residents of Dalian held a memorial ceremony at Zhugang Park to commemorate the Manchurian Incident. After the memorial ceremony, tens of thousands of citizens paraded through the bustling city.

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Today at 8:00 AM, Japanese residents of Changchun held a report ceremony and a memorial service for the fallen soldiers at the shrine to commemorate the one-year anniversary of the incident. 20,000 Japanese and Manchukuo students participated in the parade, and airplanes dropped leaflets.

Disaster Strikes Japan's Hokkaido

Epidemic Follows After the Flood

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Regarding the flood situation in Hokkaido, according to the investigation by the Ministry of Home Affairs' Social Affairs Bureau, there has been continuous heavy rain since the 4th and 5th, and the damage has affected the entire island except for Nemuro, Kushiro, and Tokachi. Agricultural products are almost completely destroyed, with at most 20% remaining. The damage is estimated at approximately 14.44 million yen. As of today, there have been 13 deaths and 12 injuries. In addition, as a result of the lack of drinking water, infectious diseases are rampant in the affected areas, and the situation is extremely tragic.

Former Japanese Railway Minister Eki Passes Away

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Former Railway Minister Eki Tsubasa passed away today. He had been suffering from pyloric stenosis and underwent surgery, but it did not improve. He had been recuperating at his private residence in Akasaka Omote-cho. His condition became critical this morning, and he passed away at 1:30 PM today at the age of 60. He was from Yamaguchi Prefecture. In the 30th year of Meiji, he graduated from the English and French Law Department of the Law School of Tokyo Imperial University. He supplemented the Ministry of Home Affairs and served as a councillor of the Kanagawa Prefecture, a councillor of the Bureau of Legislation, and concurrently as a secretary of the Cabinet. He later served as Chief Secretary of the Cabinet three times, and was also appointed as a member of the House of Peers. He earned a doctorate in law during this time. In August of the 14th year of Taisho, when the Katō Cabinet was formed, he was appointed as Minister of Justice. In July of the 4th year of Showa, when the Hamaguchi Cabinet was formed, he was appointed as Minister of Railways until the Wakatsuki Cabinet era. Later, the Wakatsuki Cabinet resigned and he went into opposition.

Den-tsu 18th, Tokyo: Eki Tsubasa, the civil administration advisor who passed away today, served as Minister of Railways in the Hamaguchi Cabinet. He and Interior Minister Adachi were considered the twin pillars of the cabinet. During the London Naval Treaty issue, he clashed with the then-Chief of Naval General Staff Kato Kanji, causing a dispute within the Privy Council. After Prime Minister Hamaguchi was assassinated at Tokyo Station, the cabinet collapsed. Hamaguchi resigned as president of the Seiyukai, and Eki introduced Wakatsuki as the party leader. He and Adachi were both considered future presidents.

Japan Sends Student Envoys to Manchukuo

The Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun says that Japanese student envoys have been selected by the National Elementary School Teachers Association, local education associations, and school principals through consultation, selecting healthy children with excellent academic performance and intelligence. Following a lottery method, fifteen student envoys, including Yamaguchi and Takano, were selected, led by principals and teachers such as Watanabe, Ueji, Yokokawa, Tamura, and Nishimura. They are scheduled to hold a group formation ceremony on the 18th and depart from Tokyo on the 19th. They will bring gifts to the Puyi couple, Zheng Xiaoxu, Mutō, and carry missions from Minister of Education Hatoyama, Minister of Colonial Affairs Nagai, and President Motoyama of the Nichinichi Shimbun.

Germany Rebuilds Its Military

A Major Threat to France

Chairman of the Disarmament Conference Goes to Geneva

Still Optimistic About the Future of the Conference

Havas 17th, Paris: In recent days, the members of the Chamber of Deputies have paid close attention to the threat of Germany's rebuilding of its military. In the afternoon, Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Herriot made a statement on this matter to the Foreign Affairs Committee of the Chamber of Deputies. Mr. Soulières, a member of the right-wing Paris City Council, will ask Herriot whether he intends to submit the file on Germany's rebuilding of its military to the negotiating parties when conducting international negotiations.

Havas 17th, Paris: Yesterday, the German Foreign Minister sent a letter to Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, stating that Germany had decided not to participate in the presidium of the Disarmament Conference in Geneva. Today, the Times in this area criticized this letter with the title "Germany and Disarmament," which reads in part, "Today's serious problem is not Germany's demand for equality in armaments, but Germany's determination to rebuild its military. Germany's determination can be seen in the recent declaration of its Minister of Defense and the memorandum that Germany sent to the French government about two weeks ago. Recently, the German government created a national youth sports organization and managed it with special mechanisms. Its purpose is to model itself directly on the Italian Fascist Youth and the Soviet Communist Youth, and to have German youth receive military training as well. This is known to everyone. From this alone, the German people's determination to rebuild their military is even more obvious."

Havas 17th, London: At 2:00 PM, Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, set off for Geneva to chair the meeting of the conference presidium on the 21st. Lord Cecil, the British representative to the League of Nations, traveled in the same car as Henderson. Before the car set off, someone asked Henderson about Germany's demand for equal rights in armaments. Henderson replied, "The presidium will immediately pay attention to Germany's notice of not participating in the disarmament work. However, I am not worried because Germany did not say in the notice that it will still pay close attention to the disarmament work, and its future attitude will change depending on the progress of the meeting. Therefore, the road to progress is not yet cut off. The responsibilities that the disarmament conference should complete are certainly not small, but if we can find a practical way to achieve universal disarmament besides the arbitration system, universal security will be achieved. I believe that mankind has now come to a fork in the road, one side being disarmament and security, and the other being competitive armament and insecurity, and the danger of war. We should decide between these two. The disarmament conference should not forget the above-mentioned reality, and when it encounters a suitable opportunity, it will lead the world into a smooth path. It is not my belief that the disarmament conference will lose its opportunity and fail."

Disarmament Proposals Cannot be Implemented

Italian Prime Minister Threatens to Withdraw from the League of Nations

Kokuminsha 17th, Rome: Italy has threatened to withdraw from the League of Nations if its proposals are not submitted for discussion at this session. According to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, what he says, he does. It is also heard that he had consulted with the former Foreign Minister and Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Grandi, and gave him strict instructions, instructing him to try to force the British government to force France to take a more tolerant attitude towards Germany's demand for equality in armaments. Therefore, political circles here have been discussing this matter in recent days. However, it is still difficult to say at this time whether Mussolini will personally go to Geneva.

Havas News Agency 18th, Rome: It has been rumored in Germany that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will personally participate in the work of the Disarmament Conference. This news has recently been officially denied.

Britain Intends to Determine Reconciliation Methods

Kokuminsha 17th, London: According to reliable sources, a formula has been drafted within Downing Street in the Prime Minister's residence, whereby the major powers will independently guarantee a large reduction in armaments in the hope of bridging the gap between Germany and the former Allied Powers. It is also heard that Britain has agreed to include Germany's demands in the disarmament convention, hoping that this solution will be accepted by all the powers and Germany. According to reports in this morning's newspapers, the British government has changed its original intention and intends to try to mediate the German-French matter without waiting for the League of Nations Council to do so at the end of this week, hoping that Germany can return to the Disarmament Conference. The aforementioned news further confirms this statement.

Important News

Anniversary of the September 18th National Crisis 5

Ma Zhanshan's Earnest Appeal to the Nation (Continued)

Ever since the violent invasion and occupation of Liaoning and Jilin by the brutal Japanese, although their representative Yoshizawa repeatedly declared to the international community that they would never undermine the territorial integrity of China, their determination to actively advance their troops and annex Jiang Province grew more urgent day by day. Initially, they used Zhang Haipeng's troops to attack, and then openly, under the pretext of protecting the repair of the Jiangqiao Bridge, they mobilized a large force of Japanese troops to approach the provincial capital. We, respecting the resolutions of the League of Nations and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, made every effort to avoid conflict, hoping to maintain world peace and prevent devastation in the region. We also repeatedly telegraphed our representative Shi to the League of Nations, urging them to reflect. However, like a ravenous boar or a long serpent, they advanced inch by inch. With the greedy ambition of wolves, they remained insatiable. Zhanshan, responsible for defending the territory, had no choice but to implement our national self-defense policy and meet them with arms. At that time, our army was filled with righteous indignation, and everyone was determined to die. They fought day and night, their spirit soaring to the clouds. However, they were ultimately defeated due to inferior weaponry, coupled with enemy planes dropping bombs on residents inside and outside the provincial city. Zhanshan, due to the appeal of the people and respecting the resolution of the League of Nations, began to withdraw his troops to the Hailun area. These are the facts of the past war with the enemy, which have been repeatedly telegraphed and announced, and I hope they will be universally acknowledged.

After withdrawing to Hailun, while actively replenishing military supplies to make a final stand, the war in Harbin broke out. Consequently, he dispatched troops to block the Japanese army stationed in Jiang from attacking Harbin, while also using the main force to assist Ding and Li, planning to connect these two armies, providing mutual support from east and west, hoping to prevent the brutal enemy's military strength from succeeding. Unexpectedly, just as our army arrived at Majiachuan Kou on the north bank of the Songhua River, Ding and Li's troops were already unable to withstand and retreated. The Japanese, detecting our army's move to aid Harbin, decided to launch a pincer attack from Qiqihar and Hailar with heavy troops, aiming to eliminate our military strength. At that time, there was a strong enemy attacking from the front, no important pass to defend in the rear, inferior weapons and ammunition internally, and isolated and cut off from aid externally. Survival was hanging by a thread. Zhanshan had been a soldier since childhood, experienced in battles, and had long put life and death aside. Considering that death can be heavier than Mount Tai or lighter than a feather, if I were to drive my loyal and righteous army to fight against the strong enemy's sharp and substantial artillery fire, the result would only be a temporary sacrifice, pleasing the enemy and further diminishing the chances of recovery. After repeated deliberation, to solve the immediate crisis, the only way was to deal with the situation as circumstances dictated, slowing down the enemy's advance, so that we could preserve our army's existing strength and wait for an opportunity to counterattack. We could also take the opportunity to investigate the Japanese's true plan to invade our territory. Therefore, I did not hesitate to risk going to Harbin to meet with the Japanese Lieutenant General Domon, using the principle of prevarication to stall them. Thus, a lifeline for the Northeast could be preserved. This is the tortuous and painful story of how Zhanshan dealt with the Japanese.

The most important thing in the international community is trust and morality. No one can rely solely on violence and fraud to gain the sympathy of civilized countries around the world. However, Japan disregards everything, risking infamy. The poison of its plans is unexpected at every turn. Now that the international investigation team is coming east soon, if I do not expose and declare to the world the various conspiracies of the Japanese that Zhanshan has personally seen and heard for more than forty days, who will know the deceitful tricks of the Japanese, and who will know that the 30 million people of our three northeastern provinces are in a hell from which there is no return? On the second

Page 8

day of February, Zhanshan, in order to understand the truth about the Japanese creating a puppet government in Manchuria, and also because of the Japanese invitation, risked going to the Liaoning Conference again. The next day, he met with the Japanese Kanto Commander Honjo, who said that most of the three northeastern provinces had been occupied by the Japanese army, and only a small part of Jilin and Heilongjiang would be difficult to resist. He hoped to cooperate with the Japanese side. That evening, he was forced to attend a meeting at Zhao Xinbo's house. All the proposals made by Zhanshan to abolish the puppet state's production were rejected by the Japanese side. On the 18th, he feigned illness and returned to Hailun. Soon after, according to Zhao Zhongren's report, on the 19th, the Japanese military headquarters forced Zhang Jinghui to establish a preparatory committee for the puppet state and ordered Zhang Jinghui and Zhao Zhongren to lead twelve puppet representatives from the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, who had been bought by the Japanese side, to Lushun to urge Puyi to be the head of the puppet state. The Japanese side instructed Puyi to decline three times, and the representatives urged him three times before completing their mission.

On March 9th, the day the puppet government was established, Zhanshan originally intended to find an excuse not to go, but in order to avoid Japanese suspicion, he had to go to Changchun. On the 10th, Komai, who is now the Director-General of the General Affairs Office of the puppet State Council, and Itagaki, the puppet high advisor, announced at the State Council meeting, by order of the Japanese military headquarters, that the puppet government would set up a General Affairs Office to manage all real political affairs of the various departments. Any political decree could not be implemented without the signature and seal of the office. On the 11th, Itagaki and Komai also announced at the State Council meeting that the Japanese military headquarters planned to have Japanese officials occupy half of the official positions in the puppet government and four-tenths of the official positions in various puppet provincial and prefectural governments in the future. For the time being, the number had been reduced, and only a hundred or so people were newly assigned to the government. Subsequently, the issue of Japanese naturalization was discussed. Xi Qia made a cautious proposal, which was severely reprimanded by Komai and Itagaki, who said that all Japanese residing in the Eastern Provinces had been exchanged for with iron and blood and should naturally be affiliated with the new country's nationality, without the need for caution. As for whether to renounce Japanese nationality, the Japanese themselves had the right to weigh it, and others were not allowed to advise.

Furthermore, it was announced that each of the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang would establish a General Affairs Office and a Police Affairs Office, all of which would be staffed by Japanese, who would control all the powers of each province. However, the General Affairs and Police Affairs offices in Jiang Province were temporarily allowed to be delayed due to Zhanshan's strong opposition, and the Japanese would take over in three months. By the 16th, Honjo came to Jiang to inspect the Dasingzhen position and said that Japan was determined, no matter what the sacrifice, never to give up the three northeastern provinces. If anyone opposed the new country, the Japanese army would be fully responsible for eliminating them. Even if a third country came out to intervene, they would declare war on them. As for political decrees, they could proceed step by step, but they had to be approved by the Japanese military headquarters stationed there. Moreover, Doihara, the head of the special service agency stationed in Harbin, and Suzuki, the brigade commander stationed in Jiang, claimed that after Japan obtained the three northeastern provinces, it had sufficient materials to make various progresses, and it would build the foundation for invading the Soviet Union to the north and resisting the United States to the east. Furthermore, it carried out an active invasion of land, transportation, finance, and education. The puppet State Council resolved: (1) All northeastern land that had already been leased out would be confiscated in full if the landowners were officials or former warlords. If the number of acres owned by ordinary people was large, half of them would be purchased at official prices. All land that had not been leased out would be confiscated by the puppet state for the Japanese government to implement immigration. (2) The Huhu-Hailun railway was the key to grain transportation in our Jiang Province. The Japanese made an agreement with Zhang Jinghui, forcing him to mortgage it for three million yuan at a price of one percent. Although the term was set for 50 years, it was tantamount to permanent occupation. They also feared that Zhanshan would not be able to accept the supplementary signature, which was sternly rejected. Recently, they have been approaching the puppet Ministry of Communications. (3) They were planning to establish a puppet Manchurian state bank, imitating the Korean bank's method, in order to manipulate finance and absorb our fat. (4) They were destroying our schools and invading our culture. All schools, in addition to stationing troops, would have all the original nationally designated textbooks at all levels that inspired patriotism deleted and revised, incorporating pro-Japanese ideas, to eliminate our national character. They were also extremely destructive of freedom of speech, even fabricating public opinion to confuse people's vision and hearing. Moreover, they were brutally murdering our intellectuals. Anyone who had been educated and had a patriotic heart was assassinated and buried alive. Former Finance Director Yan Rui, Taosuo Railway Director Zhang Kui'en, and others all suffered tragic deaths.

In summary, the Japanese ambition to annex the three northeastern provinces and destroy the world peace treaty has been openly manifested. However, they are still falsely claiming to the international community that the establishment of the new state of Manchuria is an act of self-determination by the people of the Northeast, while in reality, they are using all means of coercion and threats. The so-called public opinion is purely fabricated by the Japanese themselves. As the saying goes, "One hand cannot cover the eyes and ears of all the people in the world." This is what it means.

Zhanshan is just a warrior, lacking in knowledge, but bearing the heavy responsibility entrusted by the state and the deep trust placed in him by the people. Therefore, in recent months, he has not hesitated to risk his life alone, enduring humiliation and slander, and dealing with the national enemy with whom the Han cannot coexist, all in order to wait for the farmers to start plowing in the spring, to allow his troops to rest and recuperate a little, and then make a major move to achieve complete success. Now that the truth about the puppet state fabricated by the Japanese is clear, and the investigation team is coming east soon, it is time to seize the opportunity to instigate action. Therefore, he secretly distributed his troops in key locations and urgently came to Heihe on April 7. All important personnel from the Heilongjiang military and political offices had secretly taken the Guanfang seal to Heihe in advance and immediately resumed work as usual to plan for recovery. Although he knew that he was weak and unable to support the overall situation, his eagerness to save the country left him with no choice but to go back. He had already resolved to burn the boats after crossing the river. If he succeeded, he would be like Shao Kang with one brigade; if he failed, he would emulate Tian Heng's five hundred. As long as there was a breath left, he vowed to fight the Japanese to the end, regardless of success or failure. Alas, the country is unfortunate, and disaster arises from strong neighbors. The Baishan Mountains and Shanghai have suffered the same catastrophe. From now on, he will not return alive until he has beheaded Loulan. However, he fears that the pain of seeking compromises will not be understood by the people of the country. Therefore, he telegraphed the detailed circumstances of the intervening period to you. In the past, Zhuang Miao returned to Cao, his heart set on the Han Dynasty. Zifang assisted Liu, eager to preserve Han. Zhanshan is mediocre and foolish, and secretly admires them. Whether you know me or blame me, only the gentlemen of the country can tell. Upon reading the telegram, I am grieved and indignant, and I do not know what to say. Zhanshan, Chairman of Heilongjiang Province, bows and stamps.

Lu Army Gathered in Jiaodong 6

Fellow Townsmen in Beiping Petition for the Suppression of Liu Zhennian

Han Personally Leads a Large Army to Weixian for Deployment

Weixian Correspondence, Since the reorganization of Liu Zhennian's 21st Division in the seventeenth year of the Republic, it has been stationed in more than ten counties in eastern Shandong. Within its defense area, it has appointed and dismissed officials and collected taxes, and the provincial government has been unable to interfere. Recently, there have been rumors in the province that Liu intends to seize Weixian on a specific date. Therefore, Han Fuju, Chairman of the Provincial Government and Commander-in-Chief of the Third Route Army, personally led a large army to Weixian for deployment, and Shen Honglie's navy was guarding the coastal area of Yantai. Now, a large army has gathered in eastern Shandong, and a conflict seems imminent. The details of the events and Han's remarks are described below:

Cause of the Incident: Liu Zhennian's various actions in more than ten counties in eastern Shandong have caused considerable dissatisfaction among the local people. Recently, it was reported that the Shandong Fellow Townsmen Association in Beiping had submitted a most vehement petition to Han, enumerating Liu's crimes and requesting his suppression. At the same time, Han received a report that Liu was preparing to seize Weixian. He reported all the circumstances to the central government and requested instructions. He heard that the central government had replied by telegram, authorizing him to take action as circumstances dictated. Thereupon, he mobilized troops and began to deploy defenses. As for Liu Zhennian's office in Jinan (located at Weier Road on Jingsi Road), the director, Fu Yingxian, had already left Jinan several days ago. Yesterday (the 16th) morning, the authorities ordered it to be closed down, and only a few servants were dismissed.

Large Army Gathering: The mobilization of troops began a week

ago. It is estimated that the 22nd Division of Gu Liangmin, the 29th Division of Cao Fulin, the 81st Division of Zhan Shutang, as well as a part of the 74th Division of Qiao Lizhi, a part of the 20th Division of Sun Tongxuan, the cavalry brigade of Li Xuande, the pistol brigade of Lei Taiping, and the local militia of various counties in eastern Shandong participated, totaling approximately more than 100,000 people. Shen Honglie's navy also sailed from Qingdao to Yantai and patrolled the coast.

Han's Remarks: In recent days, a large army has gathered in eastern Shandong, with Weixian as the center. Important generals also arrived early. Commander-in-Chief Han Fuju and Chief of Staff Liu Shuxiang arrived in Weixian at 3:00 p.m. yesterday and stayed at the Weixian Chamber of Commerce. It is rumored that the vanguard has already made contact, but the authorities are still denying it. I visited Han this morning to inquire about everything. According to his remarks, Liu Zhennian has been tyrannical in eastern Shandong for more than a year. The people in eastern Shandong have long known about it. He not only controls administrative taxation, destroying Shandong's administrative system, but also plotting a rebellion. The bandits recently captured have mostly received Liu's appointment and are preparing to seize Weixian around October 10th. He is responsible for this and cannot sit idly by. Therefore, he brought people here to intercept. If they do not come to invade, he will never oppress them. If they come to invade, he will immediately defend and intercept them, and announce their crimes. Liu's troops are stationed in the areas of Dengzhou, Yexian, and Zhaoyuan. They are now 25 miles away from Changyi. My army's two brigades of Ma Guan-yi and Chen Dexin are in Changyi. There has been no contact yet. We will see if Liu has any regrets, (17th)

Details of the Case of the Yongnian Steamer's Smuggling of Opium 7

Nine Hundred and Sixty-Seven Jin of Opium

Five Hundred and Seventy-Eight Jin of Morphine

Hankou Correspondence, The Yongnian Steamer, sailing from Sichuan to Hankou, was intercepted on the 11th, when a large shipment of opium and morphine was discovered by the Customs Section of the Special Tax Office. This case, like the YuChuan Steamer smuggling case previously uncovered by the Garrison Department, is one after the other. Wang Boqun and the wife of Wang's secretary-general, Zhang Shuangqing, came to Hankou on this steamer. After the ship arrived in Hankou, Wang and others disembarked. Personnel from the Customs Section of the Special Tax Office then boarded the ship to inspect it. Liu Xieheng came forward to obstruct them, saying that these boxes were the luggage of a certain party and could not be inspected. The personnel from the Special Tax Office told them that they were ordered to search for opium. Could you prove that there was no opium in the luggage? Liu was speechless. The personnel from the Special Tax Office immediately arrested him and opened the boxes for inspection. They found drugs worth more than 100,000 yuan. At the same time, Zhang Shuangqing admitted that several pieces of jewelry in the opium box belonged to her personally. Because she was a major suspect, the Garrison Department arrested her as well. After this incident occurred, society paid great attention. General speculations were that it could not be done by ordinary opium traffickers. It is said that the scale of this opium transport was very large. The Yongnian Steamer was the first batch, and the rest all returned to Sichuan upon hearing the news. Now, the original text of the Special Tax Office's report to the Bandit Suppression Headquarters and the list of poisons are obtained and disclosed as follows:

"According to a report from Fang Shaowei, the head of the Customs Section of my office, the Yongnian Steamer, which sailed from Chongqing to Shanghai, arrived in Hankou on the eleventh of this month. I immediately ordered the search team to board the ship for inspection. Subsequently, opium and morphine were discovered in the ship's cabins and stern, totaling twenty-five boxes of various sizes. Liu Xieheng, the person who obstructed the inspection at the time, was also captured and reported to your office. Deputy Section Chief Chen arrived on the scene to supervise the transfer to your office for verification and collection. At the same time, the Second, Third, and Fourth Sections and the Supervision Office were requested to send personnel to jointly inspect the goods. The morphine, opium, clothing, and jewelry in the boxes were mixed and packed. After inspection, they were sorted, packed, and consolidated. After all the results were consolidated, there were eight boxes of morphine, fourteen boxes of opium, and two boxes of clothing and jewelry. In addition, one empty box was emptied. Seal labels were affixed and handed over to the Supervision Office for safekeeping. Liu Xieheng was sent to the Enforcement Room for detention. The matter has been reported for verification. According to this, while the verification was in progress, at 10:00 a.m. today, Deputy Officer Chen Xizeng, dispatched by your department, and Commander Ye Peng, came to the office to inspect the goods. It was found that there were a total of 360 packages in eight boxes of morphine of various sizes, 594 pieces in fourteen boxes of opium of various sizes, and 24 boxes in total with the addition of two boxes containing gold and silver jewelry. There was also one empty box. The morphine and opium were weighed together with the boxes, and the gross weight was counted. The two boxes of clothing were weighed at 91 jin together with the boxes, and the details were not counted. Subsequently, Deputy Officer Chen and Commander Ye witnessed and verified the goods, affixed seal labels, and signed their names together on the seal labels as evidence. They also opened a list of the gross weight details that they had witnessed and carried it back to submit for review. At 2:00 p.m. today, Director Zhang Nanxian of the Supervisory Office of the Party and Government Committee of your department came to the office to investigate the goods, also signed and sealed the goods, and handed them over to the Supervisory Office of my office for safekeeping. In addition to Liu Xieheng, who obstructed the inspection, being interrogated separately by my office, I respectfully submit the morphine and opium by box, with their gross weight and number, and a list of the clothes and jewelry. The details are as follows: 1. 63 packages of morphine, gross weight with box 122 jin; 2. 100 pieces of opium, 102 jin; 3. 60 pieces of opium, 66 jin; 4. 30 pieces of opium, 53 jin; 5. 69 packages of morphine, 105 jin; 6. 36 packages of morphine, 72 jin; 7. 60 packages of morphine, 94 jin; 8. 55 pieces of opium, 93 jin; 9. 28 packages of morphine, 46 jin; 10. 15 pieces of opium, 47 jin; 11. 36 pieces of opium, 98 jin; 12. 41 pieces of opium, 104 jin; 13. 11 pieces of opium, 46 jin; 14. 46 packages of morphine, 39 jin; 15. 20 packages of morphine, 32 jin; 16. 55 pieces of opium, 85 jin; 17. 32 pieces of opium, 50 jin; 18. 32 pieces of opium, 56 jin; 19. 16 pieces of opium, 27 jin; 20. 38 packages of morphine, 68 jin; 21. 80 pieces of opium, 105 jin; 22. 29 pieces of opium, 35 jin; 23. Gold and silver jewelry and clothing, 47 jin; 24. Gold and silver jewelry and clothing, 44 jin; 25. Empty box. Total: 594 pieces of opium of various sizes, 967 jin; 360 packages of morphine of various sizes, 578 jin; 2 boxes of clothing and other items, total weight with boxes 98 jin" (September 17)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 8

Rice Mill Workers Strike: There are dozens of rice mills in this city, both inside and outside the city. Farmers and businesses in the surrounding villages use them to polish brown rice for sale in Shanghai. The mills are currently in operation as it is the market season. About 140 Jiangbei workers hired by eight mills, including Jufeng Rice Mill outside the West Gate, demanded an increase in wages, as their wages were meager, with three cents of silver per stone of rice milled and one silver dollar per stone loaded onto ships. Recently, with the soaring price of foreign goods and the high cost of living, they agreed to demand an increase in wages to five cents of silver per stone of rice milled and two copper coins per stone loaded onto ships in order to maintain their livelihood. They notified the mill owners before the Mid-Autumn Festival, stating that this proposal came entirely from the workers and had nothing to do with the foremen. After receiving the report, the employers inquired with the foremen, who all claimed ignorance. Since the workers did not send representatives or go to the mills for negotiations after issuing the notice, the employers did not respond. Unexpectedly, the workers, seeing no action from the employers, went on strike unanimously at 8:00 a.m. on the 17th. The mill owners have now convened a meeting to determine a solution, and it is not known whether work will resume soon.

Anniversary of the "September 18th" National Crisis: Today marks the anniversary of the day when Japanese imperialism plundered Shenyang last year. Gloomy clouds and tragic rain have passed in the blink of an eye. The county executive committee, upon receiving a provincial order, held a commemorative ceremony. Representatives from various organizations participated, and various agencies and businesses also flew flags at half-mast to show that they will not forget the recovery of lost territory and vow to avenge the national humiliation. Entertainment venues in the city, such as the People's Grand Theater, cinemas, various bookstores, and banquets, were all closed for one day.

Fengxian 9

The Accountant of Yuanpu Farm Sent to the County for Custody: Li Yaonan, the former farm manager of Yuanpu Farm in this county, accumulated arrears of field deeds and taxes amounting to more than 8,800 yuan during his three years in office. After the new manager, Pang Derong, took over, he discovered embezzlement. After gathering the relevant local agencies for a public investigation, it was confirmed to be true. He repeatedly notified and scheduled meetings, but the former manager shirked his responsibilities and has not settled the matter to this day. Now, in order to ensure the proper handling of public funds, Manager Pang has sent the former accountant, Wang Qizhang, to the county for custody today. At the same time, he has petitioned the Songjiang Salt Transport Deputy Envoy to set a deadline for the recovery of the funds in order to complete the procedures.

Changshu 10

Skeletal Examination in the Suspected Death Case in Tianzhuang: In Tianzhuang Town, District 5 of this county, the wife of farmer Xu Guansheng, Xu Zhao, suddenly fell into the water and died last month. Without reporting the incident, the family immediately prepared for the funeral. Unexpectedly, rumors spread in the village that Zhao's death was strange, with some saying that she was beaten to death and thrown into the river, while others said that she fell into the river and died, claiming that her body was covered with bruises. As a result, villagers such as Yang Zhenmin and Yang Qiyu petitioned the county government to handle the matter impartially so that the truth could be revealed and grievances cleared. After two court hearings, both the plaintiff and the defendant held their own grounds and debated the results. Both parties requested an exhumation and examination. After approval by Examining Officer Huang, Bailiff Zhu Zhen was dispatched to the countryside to seal and cut the corners of the coffin and transport it to the city to await exhumation and examination. At the same time, the High Court was petitioned to send Examining Officer Xuanfang from the Wuxian District Court of Suzhou to Changshu. It was decided to exhume the coffin and examine it on the 17th of this month. At that time, Examining Officer Huang Jie led a full team of bailiffs to the claw climbing bay corpse field outside the North Gate, first interrogating the plaintiff and defendant one by one. After the plaintiff and defendant submitted a written guarantee, the coffin was exhumed and examined. Zhong Xuan and others examined the body for a long time, but there were still no results. The bones were then wrapped and steamed for examination on the morning of the 18th. More than a thousand people watched. The result was no injuries. The accusers, Yang Zhenmin and Yang Qiyu, were taken into custody.

Suzhou 11

Nanxin Bridge to be Rebuilt: Nanxin Bridge outside Jinmen in Suzhou is a major thoroughfare. However, the bridge has been in disrepair for many years and urgently needs to be rebuilt. The Construction Bureau designed the bridge, widening the bridge deck by one zhang and rebuilding it with steel-reinforced concrete. The estimated cost of labor and materials is more than 21,000 yuan, and it has been submitted to the Construction Department for record. After the detailed plan is submitted to the department for approval, construction can be implemented. Gongxiang in the city is the main road from Guanqian to the park, and the Construction Bureau is also planning to widen it.

Suzhou on September 18th: Yesterday was the anniversary of the September 18th National Crisis. The Wuxian County Party Department convened people from all walks of life at 9:00 a.m. to hold a commemorative meeting. The chairman was Ma Qixin, who reported on the significance of commemorating September 18th. On that day, all shops in the city flew flags at half-mast, and all newspapers suspended publication for one day. The Public Security Bureau and the Third Regiment of Military Police dispatched teams to patrol the streets and inspect suspicious pedestrians. For three days, from the 17th to the 19th, security in the city and suburbs was especially tight.

Wuxi 12

Anniversary Meeting of the September 18th: Thousands of representatives from all walks of life in the county held the Anniversary Meeting of the September 18th National Crisis at Zhongnan Theater at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. Xu Chizi, the chairman, reported on the events of September 18th last year. Wang Gongxia, Chen Chuande, Li Tiping, Hua Kun, Wang Shihen, and others then gave speeches. Next, the following proposals were passed: (1) telegraphing the central government to send troops to suppress the rebels in the Northeast; (2) telegraphing all soldiers in the country to unanimously vow to resist to the death; (3) telegraphing all compatriots in the country to unite and support the government. Finally, the meeting was adjourned with slogans. At 11:00 a.m. on the same day, all sectors of the county observed five minutes of silence to vow to avenge the national humiliation and to mourn the compatriots who died in the Northeast and Shanghai. In the afternoon, lectures were given, and the public's morale throughout the county was unprecedentedly high.

French Ancient Four Knights and the Modern French Tennis Four Knights (From Right to Left) The Majesty of Cochet, Lacoste, Borotra, and Brugnon, (Borrowed Print by Sun Linfang), fierce attacks, but their defense was too weak to support the forwards. At this time, Soviet General Mike Glorie's performance was particularly amazing, accurately passing the ball countless times to support both wings, but all missed opportunities, which was a pity. In the end, Soviet center forward Mike Glorie went straight in and broke through several lines of defense, sending the ball into the net. As a result, Scotland won a big victory 4-0. Tennis Ramblings Introducing young tennis player Sun Linfang Further Discussion of German Tennis Cartoons Here, I want to introduce a new tennis player and enthusiastic tennis fan, a beautiful young man often seen on the Chinese tennis court. His name is Sun Linfang. He went to Germany to study in 1928 and was very enthusiastic about tennis. He joined the Berlin Riviera Tennis Club as a member and received expert guidance, so his hitting posture is purely German style. He returned to China in May of this year and continued to practice at the Chinese tennis court. Now he has reached the finals of the Shanghai Grass Tennis Club Open Group B Singles Championship. His opponent is the Portuguese Sinna. He will definitely be able to easily defeat his opponent and win the championship. Although his current technique is not very refined, he has a great foundation and his future is very promising. During his years in Germany, he specialized in collecting photos of world tennis stars, either clipping them from newspapers and magazines or purchasing them from photo studios. He meticulously traced and cut out photos of postures and artistically pasted them in photo albums. He now has five or six hundred photos, a rich collection of tennis players from various countries, both male and female, old and young. He also has a hundred or so volumes of various tennis magazines. He is truly a tennis enthusiast. Last week (11th) morning, a drizzle kept falling, around 11 o'clock. Mr. Sun drove his car to my door. I squeezed into the car and we drove all the way to the Kang Luen Village on Connaught Road. We entered a delicate two-story Western-style house and stepped into a elegantly furnished living room. We sat down on the sofa. After a while, Mr. Sun brought all his collected photos and tennis books into the living room. While drinking fragrant tea and eating chocolate, we flipped through the photos, one by one. All the tennis players in the world suddenly appeared before my eyes. In addition to praising these typical tennis postures, I also admired Mr. Sun's spirit of collecting and pasting. Several cartoons clipped from German newspapers made me feel endless amusement. When Tilden invaded Berlin, he was like a fierce tiger, scaring a group of sheep in Berlin, making them run around. No one dared to compete with him. After he chased away this group of sheep, when he left Berlin, he held a racket in one hand and a lantern in the other, still looking for his opponent, but he couldn't find one, so he left proudly. There was a famous German tennis player who was always very interested in strategy. Once, he failed in a competition somewhere. When he returned home, he drew a tennis court on the table and used geometric triangles to replay the reasons for his failure. He suddenly felt that this formula was calculated incorrectly, so he suffered this defeat. When the Davis Cup was first taken away by France, the four French players sat in the Davis Cup, triumphantly returning. The players from other countries all opened their mouths wide, looking surprised. Another scene was the Davis Cup tournament. Lacoste stood on the Davis Cup arena. Below was a long ladder. Players from Britain, Germany, Italy, and other countries all fell halfway up the ladder. Only the American Tilden had climbed to the top. Lacoste happily greeted old Tilden, but in the end, old Tilden also collapsed. During the reign of Louis XIII in France, there were four very famous swordsmen. They rebelled against the Cardinal and helped the French Queen, creating earth-shattering feats and relieving the siege of Paris, bringing blessings to the French people. This is the most glorious historical event in France. In a French tennis magazine, there is a drawing of these four immortal knights, with the modern French tennis four knights Cochet, Lacoste, Borotra, and Brugnon appearing below. Their majestic and heroic demeanor truly makes people forever feel the greatness of heroes. I looked at it for a full three hours, and my head was dizzy. I still felt the endless aftertaste upon returning. I hastily jotted down these notes, hoping to amuse the readers. Local News Yesterday's National Humiliation Anniversary The whole city lowered flags in mourning and stopped entertainment All government offices worked as usual, silently vowing revenge The venue ceremony was solemn and orderly Yesterday was the "September 18th National Humiliation Memorial Day." All entertainment venues in the city were completely closed. All government agencies and shops lowered their flags to half-mast in mourning. People from all walks of life held a memorial meeting at the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps at 9:00 a.m. The military and police authorities made every effort to maintain order, which was very good. Details are as follows: Memorial Meeting of All Circles Attending Groups The groups that attended yesterday included: the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Municipal Government, the Municipal Party Headquarters, the Garrison Headquarters, the Lawyers' Association, the Accountants' Association, the General Labor Union, the Citizens' Federation, the Abolish Civil War Grand Alliance, the Women's Relief Association, the National Salvation Federation of Various Groups, the National Anti-Drug Association, the National Postal Workers' Union, and the Fifth District Cigarette, Tobacco Exchange, Pharmacy, North-South Goods, Second District Knitting, Pharmaceutical, Coal, Tenth District Cotton Textile, Sauce, Fourth District Cigarette, Postal, Fourth District Shipbuilding, Lumber Transport, First District Shipbuilding, Cloth, Qin, Water and Electricity, Ninth District Medicated Soap and other labor unions, Fresh Meat, Sand and Stone, Local Goods, Paper, Jewelry, Domestic Rubber, Brick and Tile, Flying Flower, Pawnshop, Barge Transport and other trade associations, Ai Qun, Mei Xi, Lin Yin, Ming Lun, China Vocational, Wan Zhu, Yang Zheng, Song Xue, Chong Zheng, Hui Qun, Jian Guo, Nan Qu, Shanghai Cangji, Long De and other schools, as well as more than 300 groups such as various levels of party headquarters. Representatives Zhang Taijie, Zhu Weiyao, Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, Lin Kecong, Wang Manyun, Li Yongxiang, Yuan Hongjun and others, more than 1,000 people. Strict Security The Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched the First Squadron of the Police Brigade and a small squad of armed police officers. The Municipal Government dispatched a platoon of armed police officers from the Sergeant Education Company of the Second Regiment of the Security Team to set up posts near the Youth Propaganda Corps. Tang Jinghuan, the head of the Second Sub-Bureau of the Second District, dispatched inspector Du Naiyou to lead police officers to guard the entrance of the venue. Inspectors Song Yulian, Guo Ziliang, Zhou Zhenrui and others from the Supervisory Office, and detectives Chen Guangyan and others from the Detective Team, strictly guarded and defended the venue. The strict security measures were in place from 8:30 a.m. until after the meeting adjourned at 12:00 p.m. Venue Arrangement At the entrance of the Xiaoximen Youth Propaganda Corps, a white cloth banner reading "Shanghai All Circles September 18th National Humiliation Memorial Meeting" was hung high. In the center of the stage was a portrait of the Kuomintang's General Leader. On the east side was the meeting agenda, and on the west side were the meeting slogans. The slogans on both sides were eye-catching, such as "Compatriots across the country, unite as one!", "Eliminate the puppet organization in the Northeast!", "Punish the traitors who are pro-Japanese and sell out the country!", "Expand the anti-Japanese movement and implement economic sanctions!", "Support the Northeastern Volunteer Army fighting hard against Japan!", "Work hard on political training and construction and complete local autonomy!" Although the layout was simple, it was full of a solemn and enthusiastic atmosphere. When representatives from all walks of life entered the venue, they were given black gauze when they signed in. At the same time, Jin Xing Industrial Society also presented September 18th commemorative badges at the venue. Meeting Staff Yuan Hongjun of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Li Yongxiang of the General Labor Union, Lin Kecong of the Women's Relief Association, Yu Xiji of the Accountants' Association, and other four groups served as the presidium (the Joint Association of University Professors was absent). Shi Renzheng served as the master of ceremonies, Pan Dingyuan served as the recorder, Zhang Xianfang of the Citizens' Federation, Shen Junru of the Lawyers' Association, Lu Muqin of the General Labor Union, and Zhu Yangwu and Dong Muge of the Municipal Party Headquarters served as receptionists. Zhu Xuefan and others of the National Postal Workers' Union and the local Postal Workers' Union served as marshals. Chairman's Speech The meeting began with a speech by Chairman Yuan Hongjun, who said, in brief, "Today, representatives from all walks of life are participating in this memorial meeting, and everyone feels very sad. When we recall the September 18th National Humiliation Memorial Meeting Gate (Photo taken by this newspaper's photography department) When we recall last year's September 18th, the Japanese imperialists, under the pretext of the Nakamura Incident, occupied part of our territory in the Northeast. At that time, our Northeastern army was originally going to rise up to resist and fight the Japanese imperialists to the death, but due to orders from superiors not to resist, they had to withdraw, causing the Northeast to fall. We feel even more grief and indignation. Speaking of the September 18th Incident, it was not created suddenly last year. The Japanese imperialists had long been premeditating and actively preparing in advance. We can say that from last year's September 18th to now, we have been living through the painful days of September 18th every day. The Japanese imperialists are also constantly trying to turn the Northeast into a second Korea. Today, we are holding this meeting, hoping that everyone will unite as one, work hard to resist Japan, support the Northeastern Volunteer Army, and urge the central government to recover the lost territory, so that this memorial day will be eliminated by this time next year, so as not to lose the significance of today's meeting." Representative of the Ma Clan Wu Huanzhang, the representative of the Heilongjiang Province Chairman Ma Zhanshan, also arrived at the meeting after 10:00 a.m. and took the stage to speak, saying, "Today, all circles in Shanghai are holding the September 18th Memorial Meeting here. I am extremely saddened to participate here. Today, Chairman Ma's son Kui was also prepared to participate in this meeting, but because he was not feeling well, he was unable to come. He asked me to apologize to you all. As for the situation in the Northeast, the newspapers have already reported in great detail, so I won't go into detail. I once went to Shanghai to appeal for Shanghai's assistance, and I received enthusiastic support from all walks of life. In the middle, I returned to the north due to business, passing through Vladivostok and returning to Heilongjiang Province. I was about to arrive there when I was stopped from advancing by the Russian authorities and sent back on the original ship. In this process, I left a very deep impression in my mind and gained a very big feeling in experience, understanding that in the affairs of the world, only self-reliance and self-help can gain people's help, and only self-help can resolve all difficulties. Otherwise, even if heaven does not abandon people, it is still a way to abandon oneself. Chairman Ma has now reorganized his forces and vowed to fight to the death with the enemy to regain our dignity and determined to recover the lost territory. However, with the remaining troops, limited guns and ammunition, and supplies, even if we can charge into battle and engage in hand-to-hand combat with the enemy, we still need the support of compatriots across the country to provide consistent assistance in order to sustain the situation. At the same time, today I read in the newspaper that the situation in Rehe is extremely tense. In fact, Japan has long been eyeing it, because the sea route to Vladivostok has been blocked and the first line of communication has been cut off. Now Japan is determined to occupy Rehe in order to cut off the response between our country's interior and the Northeast. Therefore, if we do not rush to rescue now, we will not be able to provide assistance even if we want to in the future. The Heilongjiang Provincial Office in Shanghai was established on the 15th of this month. I hope that all of you present, as well as compatriots across the country, will save money and food and rise up to provide practical assistance to the Northeast. We should know that protecting the Northeast is to protect North China, and it is also to protect China's territory. Please do not sit idly by and let the good opportunity to raise the Qing gauze curtain pass by in vain." Speeches from All Circles Then, Shen Junru, the representative of the Lawyers' Association, gave a speech, saying, "The September 18th Incident has been worth commemorating every day since it happened last year, because in this year, we have been in grief and pain every day. Today, all circles are holding this representative meeting. We are not just saying a few empty words to save the country. We need to start from practical actions in order to be effective. Since the September 18th Incident happened last year, there have been two attitudes from the government to the people. One is to advocate armed resistance. Now, let's observe from the international aspect. European countries have not only paid attention to the Far East issue after the September 18th Incident last year. In fact, they had already considered it at the London Conference ten years ago. When the London Conference was held, the United States paid the most attention to the Far East issue and proposed a plan to reduce the military equipment of Japan and the United States by three-fifths. At the same time, Japan also asked the United States to restrict the naval equipment in the Philippines. Therefore, the United States agreed to Japan's request. So, from the perspective of the international situation, a war between the United States and Japan is impossible at present. Even if it is possible, there is no guarantee. We see that people pay attention to the Northeast issue. We Chinese people only pay attention when the situation is so serious. Now, in this time of national crisis, we only have to break the bad habit of five-minute fever in the past, and everyone will fight persistently. We also hope that the government and the people will unite and resist to the death to be effective." Subsequently, Chen Peide, the representative of the General Labor Union, Shen Zuru, the representative of the National Salvation Federation of Various Groups, Yu Xiji, the representative of the Accountants' Association, and others successively gave speeches (the length of the speeches is omitted). Discussion of Proposals After the representatives finished speaking, they began to discuss the proposals: (1) A telegram was sent to the central government requesting it to sever diplomatic relations with Japan as soon as possible and to withdraw the ambassador to Japan and the overseas Chinese in Japan. The resolution was passed. (2) A telegram was sent to the central government requesting it to send troops to recover the lost territory. The resolution was passed. (3) A telegram was sent to the central government requesting it to withdraw from the League of Nations. The resolution was passed. (4) A telegram was sent to comfort the soldiers and civilians in the Northeast. The resolution was passed. (5) A telegram was sent to the signatory countries of the Nine-Power Treaty requesting them to safeguard peace in accordance with the treaty. The resolution was passed. (6) A request was made to the municipal government and the municipal party headquarters to unify the national salvation groups in the city. The resolution was passed. (7) A telegram was sent to the central government requesting it to order Han Fuju and Liu Zhennian to stop the civil war and unite against Japan. The resolution was passed. At the end, slogans were shouted and the meeting adjourned. It was already 11:50 a.m. Memorial Services in Various Institutions Municipal Government After receiving the telegram from the central government yesterday, the Municipal Government specially instructed all its staff to go to the government office as usual and held a memorial service at 11:00 a.m. All the staff of the Municipal Government, from the secretary-general to the section chiefs, gathered in the Municipal Government Auditorium on time. Secretary-General Yu presided over the meeting. Because the central government stipulated that the whole country should observe a five-minute silence at 11:00 a.m. to express mourning, the memorial service began with everyone standing up and observing silence. After the silence, Secretary-General Yu delivered a speech, followed by a speech by Mayor Wu. Everyone present was moved. Secretary-General Yu's Speech Today, we are holding this solemn and simple ceremony to commemorate the "September 18th" National Humiliation. I can't help but feel sad. When we recall this day last year, when we suddenly heard the news that Shenyang was occupied, we didn't believe it. Later, when the news came, we confirmed that it was true. We must know that Japan's actions were planned and premeditated, and they were not done in a day or two. We also know that Japan's aggression will never be satisfied with Shenyang alone. It will expand its scope to the important areas of the Northeast. Japan's actions in the Northeast this year can deeply convince us of this statement. As for the reasons Japan holds, it is for its own survival, that is, the lifeline that it sings loudly from top to bottom. Therefore, no matter what the situation in our country is, it will eventually take this action resolutely to satisfy its desires. Japan's actions clearly violate the League of Nations Covenant, the Nine-Power Treaty, and the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Therefore, in order to safeguard peace in East Asia and the world, our country requested the League of Nations to handle this matter fairly. After the League of Nations accepted the case, it sent an investigation team to various places in our country's Northeast and Japan to conduct on-the-spot investigations in order to seek a solution. I don't doubt the strength of the League of Nations, but I deeply feel that relying on others' help is not the way to save ourselves. Japan has resolutely and decisively recognized the puppet organization before the report has been officially published and discussed. This shows that Japan has a whole plan and will not be changed by any external interference. Therefore, no matter whether the report is biased towards our country or not, and does not straighten Japan, if we cannot unite from top to bottom to seek a way to save ourselves, I am afraid that we will not be able to wash away our shame and avenge our hatred. Looking at history, has any country declared war on another country purely for the survival of itself or for the justice of the world? Therefore, during this period of national crisis, the government should determine its diplomatic policy and defeat the enemy through negotiations with various countries. The people of the whole country should, within the scope of the law, carry out planned revenge and revenge. By this time next year, we should silently recall the achievements of a year of hard work and see to what extent we have reached. This is what I hope from my colleagues today. Mayor's Speech Today is September 18th. No one in the whole country does not feel sad, especially myself. In recent years, I have been inspecting the Northeast for a long time and have been with the people of the Northeast for many years. Now, witnessing the suffering of 30 million Northeastern compatriots, I feel even more grief and pain in terms of public affairs and private friendship. I can't directly participate in the rescue work because of my official duties, so I have more grief. In short, there are many reasons for the national crisis that constitutes today's grief, and the time is very long. Since the Sino-Japanese War of Jiawu, we have been constantly stimulated by the outside world for decades, but we still cannot make the people of the country thoroughly aware. Whether in politics, education, social economy, or production, there is still no significant progress. This is due to the neglect of the country's century-old plan. For example, China's national defense has not been established until now, and the doors are wide open, and foreigners have opportunities to seize at any time. How can we not feel pain? We must know that saving the country is the most difficult and arduous work in the world, and it cannot be done by just singing high-pitched tunes or making empty threats, nor can it be completed in the shortest time. From now on, saving the country and washing away shame requires the spirit of lying on firewood and tasting gall, and burying our heads in hard work. If the people of the whole country embrace this spirit, regardless of success or failure, profit or loss, and persevere, there will be a day to save the country. In a nutshell, the people of the whole country should do their best to fulfill their responsibilities, be loyal to their duties, and be content with their work. Those in the political circles should increase the effectiveness of their administration, so that politics will be on the right track and become more and more enlightened. Those who serve in education should do their best to educate their children, not only to cultivate the knowledge of young people, but also to cultivate their abilities. Capitalists and workers should work together carefully to make production develop and the country's resources abundant, and all supplies should not rely on imported goods. If we can do this, we can not only maintain the survival of the country and the nation, but also further save the country from danger invisibly. This is completely based on the position of the consistent joint efforts of all sectors of the country. For example, civil servants say that saving the country and recovering lost territory is the responsibility of the soldiers, while the people say that the responsibility lies with the government. This is a big mistake. In recent years, the new organizations of various undertakings in various countries have all been centered on national defense. Whether it is agriculture, industry, commerce, education, or government, they all have a certain scope. For example, when factories are established in peacetime, they are supervised by the state because they want to make ordinary production workshops in peacetime become munitions manufacturing sites when war comes. Not only factories are like this, but it is also true for agriculture and commerce. The so-called national mobilization refers to the simultaneous rise of all sectors, not just entrusting the government alone. If our country can organize in this way, the national situation can be saved. Therefore, saving today's national crisis depends on everyone's efforts and each person fulfilling their share of responsibility. I often encourage myself to do my duty and abide by my duties. On this painful memorial day, I especially express this statement and hope to encourage all my colleagues in the government. First of all, the people of the whole country must fulfill their national duties, make consistent efforts, unite and struggle, and then can we be effective. Chairman Chen Chengshi reported on the summary of the "September 18th" National Humiliation. The following telegrams were passed: (1) A telegram was sent to the whole country vowing to recover the lost territory and resist the violent Japanese. (2) A telegram was sent to the League of Nations requesting it to make a fair resolution on the Northeast Incident as soon as possible and to take drastic and effective measures to stop the violent Japanese aggression. (3) A telegram was sent to the soldiers of the whole country to unanimously vow to resist and defend themselves. (4) A telegram was sent to the central government requesting it to immediately order the suppression of the Northeast rebels. Cai Jinghai, Zhang Yunhe, Chen Pin and others then successively gave speeches and shouted slogans to dismiss the meeting. The Whole City Flew at Half-Mast Yesterday, all organs, schools, factories, shops, etc. in the city flew at half-mast in mourning. Therefore, although the national flag of the Republic of China with the blue sky, white sun, and red ground was flying on all the roads, it was dim and dull, and it felt even more bleak. Amusement places such as the Great World, the Small World, the Fairy World, the New New Rooftop Garden, Yong'an, Tianyun Tower, Xianshi Paradise, and Qitian, Tianchan, Yixing, Penglai, etc., as well as Central, New Central, Fu'an, Empire Guanghua, Jiuxing, Shanxi, Zhabei, Beijing, Golden, Southeast and other cinemas, all stopped business, the iron doors were closed, and it was marked "September 18th National Humiliation Memorial Day Closed for One Day." Various museums also stopped publishing various entertainment advertisements for one day in mourning. Special Martial Law in the Whole City Chinese Boundary In the Nanshi, Zhabei, Wusong, and Huxi districts, all police stations were ordered to impose martial law. All important roads were guarded by double posts. Inspectors, detectives, and female inspectors were all dispatched to inspect pedestrians. Armed police officers of the police brigade were stationed in various posts, and the car patrol team patrolled with arms. The most stringent areas were Xiaodongmen, Ximen, Laobeimen, Xieqiao, Public Sports Ground in Nanshi, Tanzhiwan, Chihama Bridge, Xinzha Bridge, Tiantongan Station, North Railway Station in Zhabei, Caojiadu, Zhoujiadu in Huxi, Lanndidu and Lujiazui in Pudong, and Paotaiwan in Wusong. On Longhua Jinyilu and Longhua Road, armed soldiers from the Garrison Headquarters set up sentry posts. At Gaochang Temple, soldiers from the Navy Department Guard Battalion were stationed. Near the Municipal Government and Xieqiao and Xuxie Roads, the security team was stationed and inspected pedestrians very strictly. The security teams in each district were dispatched with arms to patrol, and the security was very strict. Gong Xikui, the superintendent of the Public Security Bureau, also personally inspected Nanshi at 11:30 a.m. and Zhabei at 1:30 p.m. The situation was very peaceful. Concession Area All French Concession police stations, Chinese and Western detectives, were dispatched with arms. Posts were added to all important roads. The iron doors at the junction of the Chinese and Concession areas, such as Xiaodongmen, Xinbeimen, Laobeimen, Xiaobeimen, Nanyang Bridge, and Xieqiao, were completely closed, leaving only side doors for pedestrians. Chinese and Western patrolmen were stationed at each door to conduct strict inspections. Piles of barbed wire were piled up at the junction of Lujiawan and Dapu Bridge, and only Fenglin Bridge and other places were opened to allow vehicles to pass. Detectives were stationed everywhere in the Great World and Dongxinqiao. All Chinese and Western detectives from the police stations in the Public Concession were dispatched. Detectives were armed and stationed at the border to inspect pedestrians. Armed Chinese and Western patrolmen were stationed at various important roads such as Nanjing Road and Edouard Road, and the police cars patrolled. Detectives patrolled and stayed on standby. Security was especially strict in Yangshupu in Hudong and Caojiadu in Huxi.

From the Hongjiang Road intersection to the Park Shooting Range, it was originally a Chinese territory, but because the headquarters of the Japanese Marine Corps and the headquarters of the military police were stationed there, the section was used as a Japanese military alert area. At the time, only three or five workers were seen passing by in groups and were dispersed.
