The Authority of Tan Dog No. 21 Zhan Lu

The news material about the death of the dog star Zero Din occupies a huge space in the newspaper; Alas! Can a person be inferior to a dog? This is called the authority of the dog. The glorious history of dogs is too numerous to mention. There are dogs who serve the Red Cross Society and help starving people in the snow; there are dogs who serve in the police station and detect huge thieves; and there are countless loyal dogs who are rumored to have rescued their masters in distress at home and abroad, seemingly more than the loyal men in the world.

I remember a certain pen record that the authority of dogs is better than doctors:

The dog kept by a certain family understood the properties of the medicine because the owner had been ill for a long time; every time after the doctor prescribed the medicine, the dog would sniff the medicine bag; if the medicine was right, the dog would show joy and wag its tail. If the medicine was not right, the dog would bark a few times, hold the medicine bag in its mouth, and throw it into the trash can. The owner was able to recover from his illness gradually because he depended on the dog, and he was not mistaken by the incompetent doctor who prescribed the wrong medicine.

I also remember a foreign magazine recording that the authority of dogs is better than matchmakers:

There is a strange custom in Serbia. All the girls who have reached adulthood choose a good day in spring and autumn to have a dinner party together; when the banquet is withdrawn, everyone puts the leftover meat bones on the table and orders the dog to chew it; whoever's meat bones the dog chews first, that person will be the first to marry; who is the second, who is the third, and who is the last, everyone listens to the dog who chews the bones and determines the order of the marriage period, and no one dares to disagree.

I feel here: If the dogs raised are all like this, then there will be no murderous quack doctors in society, and there will be no runaway girls who oppose matchmakers. Retrospective of September 18th Xu Bai'an

(1) The past is like a dream!

I still remember clearly: when the news of the September 18th Japanese soldiers' atrocities reached Shanghai last year, we were eating soup noodles in a small restaurant near the school. Everyone was surrounding a newspaper from the 19th, nervous and calm, indignant and silent. In the dizzy eyes, there were shocking headlines, such as Japanese soldiers bombing Beida Camp, Zang Shiyi and Rong Zhen being abducted, Wang Yizhe, the brigade commander, being killed, the Bank of Communications being robbed,... the eyes were not only dizzy, but they were almost shooting out sparks! After that, there were grandly held citizen rallies, the establishment of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, the organization of donation teams, everything, everything, was carried out enthusiastically and jumping wildly.

(2) How can I recall it?

Although the land of Northeast China has been ravaged almost entirely by the claws of the tyrannical Japanese, the millions of people across the country are using their best efforts, hoping to defeat the tyrannical Japanese and recover the lost land outside the pass. However, General Zhang Xueliang, who held the military power, refused to step out of the pass. During this period, the Japanese soldiers also came to Songhu to start the 1.28 massacre. Although they had suffered losses from the defense and attacks of the brave 19th Route Army soldiers, the shooting of those huge bombs, the destruction of incendiary bombs, the broadcasting of bombs, the fire in Zhabei, the destruction of countless houses, the tragic death of many residents, the loss of property,... All of this is naturally the Japanese people's iron-like crimes, the records of atrocities that cannot be torn down, but it is also the shame of our great Chinese nation that is difficult to煎洗, because our government ultimately lacks determination, and the anti-Japanese soldiers finally retreated due to the lack of support.

(3) What about the present?

Now, the autumn wind is萧飒, and in a blink of an eye, it is September 18th again. The Northeast has fallen into the hands of the enemy for exactly one year today. And just three days ago丨the Mid-Autumn Festival in the old calendar, the political warlords and capitalist officials manipulated by Japan on that day actually brazenly and absurdly formally recognized the puppet Manchuria they created! Although the League of Nations can also裁制 this absurd move, and the signatory countries of the Nine-Power Treaty can also correct it, it is not guaranteed. In this day and age, except for intervening for the sake of their own conflicting interests, no one is willing to be a fool to speak out for justice and say public words to redress grievances. To save China, only our people themselves! To recover the lost land, we can only rely on our own loyalty, bravery and sacrifice! Arise, friends whose hearts have not died! Arise! Go to the outside of the pass together! Pillow Notes Huo Xueming

The sigh of the琴絃 broke the silent Tianye. I realized it only after waking up. But I was still lying in bed, motionless. The tears of a Korean wandering musician must be in the moonlight again; his eyelashes were wet from gazing at his homeland.

This musician is a mute. He doesn't speak all day long. But the mystery of his emotions, relying on sound, will be read in my heart every night, the soul, and even the vast and silent sea. But I was lying in bed, without a word to comfort him, or material aid. "Sympathy" is just an uncashed expired check.

I am sick, and dark clouds are wandering in front of me. But my heart is like a snake, it coils and bites in my blood, and I feel pain.

Maybe one day I will wander to the north of the forest and the sea with a Chinese pipa? At this time, the dumb Oriental lion will die! The Death of Shi Chen Wei

After the Reduction of Political Expenses in Hubei Province 18

The Education Sector Demands Exemption from Reduction

Submitting Reasons to Commander-in-Chief Chiang

(Hankou Correspondence) Hubei Province's financial expenditure is in deficit, with accumulated debts of political and educational expenses totaling 3,041,249 yuan. Combined with various loans, the total deficit amounts to a staggering 15,216,512 yuan. This time, the Commander-in-Chief's headquarters stipulated that monthly political and educational expenses should not exceed 700,000 yuan. After repeated deliberations by the provincial government, it was decided to reduce the budget from 1,094,071 yuan to 862,580 yuan, implementing a policy of reduction and consolidation. The government side is still enduring the pain to maintain the situation, but the education sector has already risen in opposition. Educational funding has already been reduced three times in recent years. The current expenditure of 276,650 yuan has reached the point where it cannot be reduced any further. If the provincial government's decision to implement a new budget with an 80% reduction, reducing it to 221,320 yuan, is carried out, it will be impossible to maintain educational affairs. Moreover, the recent accumulation of unpaid educational expenses, which have not been issued for June, has caused great panic in the lives of principals, faculty, and staff of various schools. If further reductions are made, they will be left starving. Therefore, representatives were elected some days ago to petition the provincial government, requesting that the status quo be maintained. On the afternoon of the 14th, at 4:00 PM, Chen Dejiong, Xia Zhengsheng, Wang Yizhou, and Tian Yisheng were selected to bring a petition to Commander-in-Chief Chiang's headquarters to present their difficulties. Chiang sent acting Chief of Staff Zhu Shaoliang to receive them. First, Chen Dejiong, representing the entire education sector, expressed deep appreciation for Chiang's successful suppression of the Red bandits. He then presented three points: (1) Education in Hubei has been reduced three times in the 17th, 20th, and 21st years [of the Republic], which is only one-third of the level in provinces such as Jiangsu and Zhejiang. Recently, there have been six months of accumulated unpaid expenses, and the difficulties have reached an extreme point. (2) The budget for educational institutions is inherently less generous than that of administrative agencies. Furthermore, administrative agencies can be reduced and consolidated simultaneously, while educational institutions cannot be reduced or consolidated; only reductions are possible. Given the magnitude of the accumulated unpaid expenses, there is virtually no room for further reduction. The headquarters previously instructed the provincial government to reorganize Hubei's finances, emphasizing the importance of maintaining both education and security while practicing thrift. Although the provincial government has slightly different reduction standards for educational and administrative expenses, items such as overseas study fees, boarding fees for normal school students, subsidies for orphans, and internship fees cannot be reduced in practice. Moreover, the operating expenses of various schools are already very meager. With the current high prices, further reductions will make it impossible for schools to operate. (3) The Executive Yuan's 53rd meeting resolved that centrally administered educational and cultural institutions would receive full payments starting in July. Commander-in-Chief Chiang's order to the provincial government to reduce political expenses also shows a special intention to protect education. He requested that the original intention of protection be upheld and that Hubei's educational expenses be approved based on the budget approved by the Hubei Provincial Government in the 20th year [of the Republic], without further reductions, so that Hubei's educational undertakings could maintain their current status. After Chen's statement, acting Chief of Staff Zhu Shaoliang replied, promising to forward it to Commander-in-Chief Chiang for consideration. (September 14th)

National Central University Expands Library Plan 19

Luo Jialun, President of National Central University, announced before taking office his plan for the university. The first step is a period of stabilization, followed by development. Now that the organizations of various departments and faculties are in place, it has entered a period of stability. The future development plan is to first expand the library. The current university library only lends books to university faculty, staff, and students. The future plan is to expand the library and open it to the public, allowing scholars who are seeking professional development to have access to reading opportunities, and improve Chinese culture. The second is to expand the campus to Beijige, such as using the viewing platform to cooperate with the astronomy department, and other plans. Although it is related to funding, having these goals will ensure it will be achieved one day.

Thirteen Men and Women

According to the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, as of recently, it has approved subsidies for thirteen self-funded students studying in Japan, including twelve males and one female. Anhui Education Department Promulgates Measures for Mobile People's Schools 21

(Anhui News) The Anhui Education Department yesterday promulgated measures for the establishment of mobile people's schools attached to various educational institutions in order to popularize the literacy movement. The twelve measures are as follows: (1) Purpose: The temporary purpose of mobile people's schools is to popularize literacy education among the people. (2) Name: The name of mobile people's schools attached to various educational institutions should be prefixed with the name of the attached institution. (3) Equipment: In addition to desks and chairs, the following items must also be provided: 1. Small blackboard, 2. Chalk, 3. Paper, 4. Loose-leaf textbooks, 5. Enlarged textbook charts. (4) Qualifications: Anyone, whether literate or not, may register for admission. A volunteer application must be completed upon admission. (5) Teachers: Staff members designated by the educational institution will serve as teachers. Teachers will be given appropriate subsidies. (6) Teaching Materials: Based on the occupational needs of the general public and their level of education, select individual characters and phrases to compile the text of the lesson, print loose-leaf textbooks, and enlarge and print each lesson into charts. (7) Teaching Method: Adopt a completely individualized teaching method. Learners go to the teacher daily to receive new characters and lesson text. The time of day is optional, and the teacher decides the amount of instruction. Those with low intelligence can read one lesson at a time, while those with high intelligence can read two or three lessons at a time. Before reading a new lesson each time, the teacher must examine whether the lessons already read have been mastered. Those who have not mastered the material must review it; no new lessons will be taught. (8) Practice: After returning home each day, students must practice writing and making sentences and submit them to the teacher for review. The teacher will first give the practice topics. (9) Testing: Student learning, the value of teaching materials, and the gains and losses of teaching methods must be tested frequently in order to improve them at any time. (10) Examination: Divide all teaching materials into several stages, and hold an examination once each stage is completed. (11) Graduation: Those who have completed all the textbooks and passed the examination will be allowed to graduate and will be issued a certificate. (12) Supplementary Provisions: These measures may be amended at any time if there are any omissions. (September 14th)

Yesterday at Various Schools 22

Commemorating "September 18th"

Fudan University: Military officer Mr. Guo of Fudan University and students Kong Lingjue, Wu Tiesheng, and others, in view of the fact that the Northeast Volunteer Army is loyal and brave in resisting Japan and urgently needs supplies, contacted the entire student body to fast for one day yesterday and donate all the money saved from meals to the Volunteer Army. It is said that many people joined the fast, so the amount was considerable.

Jianguo Middle School: All teachers and students of Jianguo Middle School yesterday expressed their profound grief over the September 18th National Humiliation Day. In addition to sending representatives Hu Yuemei and Lu Tingjian to participate in the commemoration meeting of various circles, a commemorative ceremony was held in the school hall at 9:00 AM, presided over by the acting principal of the school, Yuan Yeyu. Mr. Chen Binhe was introduced to give a detailed speech on Sino-Japanese relations and the current situation in the Northeast. Teachers Wang Zhongcan and Ruan Xingzhi, and students Li Bingnian, Luo Guangrong, and Xu Guoqing gave speeches with solemn words, which moved the audience. Finally, Mr. Chen Dezheng of the school asked the students two questions: "Who will wash away the national humiliation?" and "Who can eliminate our current enemy, Japan?" All the students rose up and answered loudly, shouting, "We will!" and then silently mourned for five minutes in tears. After the meeting, all the students went to the classroom to write essays on the topic "How to Deal with Our Enemy." No students asked for leave to go out all day.

Shanghai Girls' High School: Shanghai Girls' High School held a September 18th Commemorative Meeting at the People's Education Museum Auditorium in the Wenmiao at 9:00 AM yesterday, attended by more than 300 teachers and students from the entire school. First, Principal Wu Zhiqian presided over the meeting and reported on the events of September 18th. Then, Director of Instruction Gong Yuyi gave a speech on the students' understanding of September 18th and the true meaning of studying without forgetting to save the country. Finally, Xiang Guozhong gave a speech on the events of the September 18th National Humiliation Day and our tools for saving the country in the future. The gathering was full of solemn air, and everyone was furious, determined to eliminate the enemy. The national spirit is immortal, and the shame of the country will soon be avenged. It is also said that in order to intensify their work and practice studying without forgetting to save the country, the school continued to hold classes as usual in the afternoon.

Nanyang Advanced School of Commerce: Nanyang Advanced School of Commerce held a September 18th National Humiliation Commemorative Meeting in the school auditorium at 9:00 AM yesterday, attended by more than 400 faculty, staff, and students. Principal Wu Xinglian and teachers Wu Jiangleng, Mao Xiao Cen, Chen Qiyu, Zheng Huiyi, and student Jiang Tongshan gave very solemn speeches. Finally, everyone shouted various slogans, which was extremely tragic.

East China Girls' School: The number of students in the Girls' Department of East China Middle School has increased sharply this semester, and their spirits are even more invigorated. Yesterday was the commemoration of the September 18th National Humiliation Day. The school followed the order of the Municipal Education Bureau and held classes as usual. A national humiliation commemoration meeting was held at 11:00 AM, attended by more than 100 teachers and students from the entire school. First, Principal Ma Laizhen presided over the meeting and reported on the significance of the commemoration. Then, Dean of Academic Affairs Liu Zhengxiao gave a speech on the students' understanding of the national humiliation commemoration.

Vocational Education Society Fasts to Help the Volunteer Army 23

Since the China Vocational Education Society initiated the monthly donation from salaries to support the Northeast Volunteer Army, and abstained from lunch on September 18th to donate the saved food expenses to help the compatriots in Northeast China who were in distress, letters of approval and donations have poured in from all sides. Mr. Wang Qizhang, a famous doctor in this city, sent a letter to the association expressing his views, which were published in yesterday's newspaper. The association has now received a letter from Mr. Mu Ouchu, a leader in the industrial and commercial sector and a director of the association, stating that he strongly approves of the two methods initiated by the association and has already implemented them separately. From now on, he will save 30 yuan per month from household food expenses to support the Northeast Volunteer Army until the lost territory is recovered. Since Japan recognized the puppet state of Manchuria, its ambition to annex has been completely exposed. All Chinese people are indignant and determined to resist permanently, so that the enemy's schemes will not succeed, and the lost territory will eventually be recovered. This is the responsibility of all Chinese people. The Northeast Volunteer Army has risen up to resist and has repeatedly thwarted the enemy's advance. If all patriots, like Mr. Mu, practice thrift and actively support them, then recovering the lost territory will not be difficult.

Zhejiang Sericulture Vocational School Visits Shanghai 24

The Zhejiang Provincial Advanced Sericulture Vocational School, formerly the West Lake Sericulture School, has been reorganized and has a history of nearly forty years. It is the most historical and successful school in China's vocational education. This time, about 30 senior students of the school, led by Xu Haofang, Director of General Affairs and Specialist Teacher, and teacher Sun Boyou, plan to visit the silk situation in the Shanghai area. They arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, and important silk agencies in the city, such as the Ministry of Industry, the Commodity Inspection Bureau, the Raw Silk Inspection Office, and the China United Sericulture Improvement Association, have all been visited. Last night, they also visited the printing and editing departments of this newspaper. They are said to be departing this morning to visit Suzhou, Wuxi, and other places, and then transfer to Zhenjiang and Nanjing for inspection.

Creating New Facilities for Middle School 25

Chuangzhi Middle School on Fuxu Road in this city has been working hard for years to meet the needs of society, expanding its school buildings, adding a girls' department, helping women who have dropped out of school, and establishing a women's people's school. It is now recognized that the past mistakes of vague education have been made, and efforts are being made to remedy them by purchasing various specimens, charts, and graphs to develop the true meaning of textbooks. The management is both lenient and strict, and students' thoughts and behaviors are corrected at any time and place, so as to become outstanding individuals. The teachers and students are full of energy and pleasure. It is recently heard that the school authorities want to implement their proposals and have specially formulated free student, half-fee student, and preferential treatment measures to promote the popularization of education.

First Act of the International Football Tournament 27

Scotland Wins Big Against Ireland

Ireland's Strong Defense Ineffective

Scotland's Center Forward Shows His Skills

Belfast, Scotland, 17th (Reuters) In front of 40,000 spectators today, Scotland defeated Ireland 4-0 with excellent football skills. This is the first act of this season's International Football Tournament.

Scotland's Lineup: (Goalkeeper) McClarn, (Defenders) Grant, (Center Backs) Klafene, Jones Easton, Tweef (Forwards) Crawford, Stephenson, McGregor Leith, McFee, King

Ireland's Lineup: (Goalkeeper) Scott, (Defenders) Cork, Folden, (Center Backs) Farleyon, Jones, Gaotai (Forwards) Mikel, Presdre, English Miller Kai Lai

Excellent Goalkeeping by the Irish Team: Although Irish goalkeeper Scott repeatedly displayed his goalkeeping skills, the sharpness of the Scottish forwards was extraordinary, repeatedly breaking through the center back line. Their victory was largely due to this. Two minutes into the game, Scotland's left wing King received a pass from Crawford and immediately scored the first goal.

Halftime Score 2-0: The Scottish forwards continued to put pressure on and ravaged the Irish defense line, but could not break through Scott's goal. However, the Irish left wing Kai Lai fiercely shot, but was saved by goalkeeper McClarn. This ball did not go in. Scotland's McFee dodged Cork and scored the second goal. At halftime, the Scottish team led 2-0.
